 IANS
 In 2006, after doing engineering from a private engineering college in Noida, Aditya Singh of Bijnor district and Anand Singh of Patna started working as a software engineer in "accenture" in Bangalore and Saurabh Mishra "infosys" of Kannauj
 us vakt tak teenon ek-duusare ko jaanate tak na the
 We were all of the same age, but all three had the same passion for environmental protection
 padhai ke saath-saath paryaavaran sangrakshan ke liye yojit hone vaale kaaryakramon main teenon lagaataar bad-chadhakar hissaa lete the
 Aditya, Anand and Saurabh became good friends of each other through such programs
 vahi vah samay tha jab maharashtra ke vidarbha main kapaas kii kheti karne vaale kisaanon kii aatmahatya ke aankade bhi bad rahe the
 These incidents were disturbing to all three
 teenon ne milakar gaharaai se padtaal kii to pataa chalaa ki khudakushi karne vaale kisaan choti jot ke the
 Due to more and more use of pesticides and fertilizers to increase the yield, farmers went under the burden of debt and would die in respect of dignity
 duusari ore vidarbha main hi kuch kisaan puri tarah jaivik kheti ke jariye kapaas kii paidaavaar kaa niryaat karke apni aay badha rahe the
 Aditya, Anand and Saurabh wondered why not make a market in the country for the farmers of organic cotton or organic cotton of Vidarbha
 uske baad teenon ne naukari chhod di or april, 2012 main green organic clodin privet limited naam kii company banaai, jiskaa daftar uttar pradesh main gajiabad jile ke vaishali main kholaa gaya
 It was the first company to produce organic cotton fabrics in the country
 saurabh bataate hai, ''duniya bhar main bharat main sabase zyada organic coton kii paidaavaar hoti he lekin puraa maal duusare deshon main bhej diya jaataa he
 Why can't we wear good when we can grow good
 " isi soch ko saamne rakhkar teenon doston ne korporate, shiksha, aatithy (hospitality), retail kshetron main organic coton se bane kapadon kaa bazaar talashna shuru kiya
 Started in the corporate sector
 aditya bataate hai, ''hamen yah pataa tha ki kai korporate companiyaan khaas maukon par apane karmchaariyon ko tarah-tarah ke tohfe bhi detii hai jinamein tii-shart yaa shart vagairah bhi shaamil hai
 "so over two dozen companies were contacted but the success was achieved in July 2013, a year later
 indigo airlines ne saatvin varshganth ke liye ''green organic cloding privet limited" ko jaivik kapaas kii bani 7,700 tii-shart kaa order diya
 At that time, Rajalakshmi Cotton Mill in Kolkata was the largest exporter of organic cotton fabrics in the country
 kai daur kii baatcheet ke baad aditya, anand or saurabh rajalakshmi coton mil ke maalik rajat jaipuria ko desh main hi aapurti karne ke liye ek hi tarah kii dizin vaali 7,700 tii-shart banane ke liye raji kar paae
 Rajat Jaipuria started manufacturing T-shirts with the same design from organic cotton at his factory in Junglepur Industrial Area, Kolkata
 isi samay brand ''aai em greeni" launch kiya gaya
 Indigo was supplied a T-shirt within a record three weeks
 iske baad rajalakshmi coton mil unki sahyogi ban gai
 This was the turning point
 iske baad ''green organic cloding privet limited" ko google, wales fargo bank, canan jaisi companiyon ke order mili
 The company of these three friends was challenged the most by coca-cola
 coca cola apane saath sirf unheen vendor ko jodta he jo vishwa stareey ''saplir guidelins principal" (esajeepi) ke maanakon par khare utarate hai
 Rajalakshmi Cotton Mill made several changes to the factory in terms of safety and quality to SGP standards
 ek varsh baad ''green organic cloding privet limited" esajeepi ke maanak puraa karne vaali desh kii pehali company bani
 It also became the first company in the world to supply organic cotton clothing to coca-cola
 korporate sector main dhak jamaane ke baad 2014 main aditya, anand or saurabh ne shiksha ke kshetra main pravishthi kii yojana banaai
 "we came to know that threads made of bamboo fibers destroy germs," explains Anand
 china kii ek company se bans ke reshe se bane dhaage kharidkar vishwaprasiddh brand ke liye mojey banane vaali gujarat kii ek company se mojey banawaye
 "aditya, Anand and Saurabh wore these socks for the entire three months and found that despite being dirty they did not smell at all
 in khaas mojon ke liye ''smel free" brand launch kiya gaya
 In order to find a market for this, first contact was made in Mayo College, Ajmer
 yah college hostel main rahane vaale chaatro ke mojon se aane vaali badboo se pareshaan tha
 Mayo College immediately ordered one thousand smel free socks
 aaj har maheene 30,000 jode mojey desh ke sabhi bade boarding skool main bheje ja rahe hai
 Encouraged by these results, it is now ready to supply T-shirts and shirts made of bamboo thread for school students
 mojon kii safalataa ke baad punjab kii ek factory se samjhauta karke desh main pehali baar bans ke dhaage se bane tauliyon ko bazaar main utaara gaya
 Despite being thinner than a common towel, it absorbed more water than them
 in khoobiyon ke kaarangreen organic cloding privet limited spa ke kshetra main vishwa ke sabase bade brand sicks sences ko bans kaa tauliya supplai karne vaali vishwa kii akeli company ban gai

 desh main maujuud sabhi online companiyaan is vakt uske brand bech rahi hai
 Now the next goal is to deliver clothes made of organic cotton and bamboo fiber to every corner of the world within a year, for which a trio of Aditya, Anand and Saurabh have been mobilized

 '50 anguliyaan haathon kii, 50 anguliyaan pairon kii, or chah dil ek saath dhadak rahe hai
 
 
 That's what Facebook said on 26-year-old Kimberley Tucci when five children were born together, 'surprising' them at their home
 
 
 janvari main janme in bacchon ko haal hi main ek behad khubasurat photoshute ke jariye duniya ke saamne pesh kiya gaya, jo is vakt viral ho rahaa he
 
 
 Had to happen
 
 
 aisa bhi nahin he ki 28 janvari, 2016 ko kimberli or won tuki (vaughn Tucci) ke ghar main janme tiffeni (tiffany), penelopi (penelope), beatrix (beatrix), eli (allie) or kith (keith) ne internet par aane waalon kaa man janm ke baad hi moh liya ho
 
 
 In fact, he has been seen among Internet users since before his birth, when he reached Kimberly's womb, as the Tucci couple have maintained a page on Facebook - Surprised by Five (surprised by Five - Surprised by Five), on which he has uploaded all the information and photos related to Kim's pregnancy and the birth of children
 
 
 kimberli tathaa won pehle se do betiyon ke mata-pita the, jab unhone tisare bachche kii yojana banaai
 
 
 When Kimberly became pregnant, 'mummy-papa' was shocked to find out that he was going to be the parent of five children - four daughters, one son - this time not one or two
 
 
 tabhi se kimberli or won sabhi kuch - pregnancy test, sonogram, apni bhavanaaen, apane dar - duniya ke saath fasebuk par baantate aa rahe hai
 
 
 Now that the children have arrived in the world, their first and very captivating photoshoot has forced all the viewers to 'sigh'
 
 
 vaise, kimberli kii daadi ne bhi ek 'go fund' pej banaaya he, taaki logon se madad kii apil kar saken, taaki saat bacchon ke mata-pita ab ek vine kharid len, jisamen baithkar sara parivaar ek saath kahin aa-ja sake
 
 
 The comments agar aap is parivaar ke bare main isse bhi zyaada jaankaree paanaa chaahate hai, to neeche gaye post ko padhie
 
 
 It is not that Tiffany, Penelope, Beatrix, Allie and Keith were born on the Internet on January 28, 2016 in the house of Kimberly and Vaughn Tucci
 Those who have become fascinated after birth
 
 
 darasal, ve apane janm ke pehle se hi, jab ve kimberli ke garbh main pahunche the, internet yuzaron ke bich dekhe jate rahe hai, kyonki tuki danpati ne fasebuk par ek pej bana rakhaa he - sarpriced bai five (paanch se hairaan - Surprised by Five), jis par unhone kim kii garbhavastha or bacchon ke janm se judi sari jaankaree or tasviren aplod kar rakhi hai
 
 
 Kimberly and Vaughn were already parents to two daughters when they planned a third child
 
 
 jab kimberli garbhvatee hui, to 'mummy-papa' ko hairaan karne vaali soochna mili ki vah ek yaa do ke nahin, is baar paanch-paanch bacchon ke mata-pita banane ja rahe hai - chaar betiyaan, ek betaa
 
 
 Since then, Kimberly and Vaughan have been sharing everything - pregnancy tests, sonograms, their emotions, their fears - with the world on Facebook
 
 
 ab jab bachche sansar main aa chuke hai, to unke pehle or behad manamohak photoshute ne sabhi dekhne waalon ko 'aahen bharne' par majaboor kar diya he
 
 
 By the way, Kimberly's grandmother has also created a 'go Fund' page to appeal to people for help, so that parents of seven children can now buy a van, in which the whole family can sit and move together
